preregistered scoring campaign has not yet run.

## D9a percent-decode primary score: default Whitefoot wins, facts neutral (2026-07-12)

The one preregistered campaign completed without rerun: 30 fresh processes,
all 90 samples retained, 256 MiB fixed corpus, AC power identity stable, and no
recorded power/thermal transition (the thermal probe was consistently
unavailable).  Median throughput was 629.484 MiB/s Whitefoot facts-on, 620.343
MiB/s facts-off, and 383.456 MiB/s shipped Rust.  The paired facts-on/Rust
median ratio is 1.6533 with stratified bootstrap interval [1.6309, 1.6668]: a
predeclared **meaningful Whitefoot win**.  Facts-on/facts-off is 1.0100 with interval
[1.0047, 1.0196], inside the ±2% **practical parity** band.

Attribution matters: facts-on and facts-off proof reports are byte-identical,
with all six bounds sites retained and none proved.  This is therefore not a
proof-elision win.  It is the intended default-floor result: the first green
low-tier-AI Whitefoot shape beat the ordinary released `percent-encoding` 2.3.2
public-iterator path.  Post-result assembly shows the Rust adapter making an
out-of-line `PercentDecode::next` call per yielded byte while the Whitefoot helpers
fold into one call-free loop.  Expert Rust could plausibly close that gap with
inlining/LTO/restructuring, but those are ceiling experiments and cannot alter
this primary score.  Canonical evidence and caveats are in
`experiments/default-floor/percent-decode/RESULTS.md`; raw SHA-256
`a659855f0d3fa909874f861f6d7ec7401653a877a7c0bd0d1544d4333054324b`,
analysis SHA-256
`24cfe1e9a3aed9d647d7ae9f684f178fe62c363bff1afa405a1dc245376bd5b9`.

D9a is satisfied for this target, not generalized.  The next evidence step is
one independently preregistered shipped-library replication; an optional
post-primary Rust inlining ceiling may explain mechanism but is not required
to preserve the default-floor conclusion.

## D9a utf8parse replication preregistered (2026-07-12, before generation)

The second shipped-library target is frozen independently against ordinary
`utf8parse` 0.2.2 defaults and its public `Parser`/`Receiver` API.  The one-shot
task maps valid scalars and invalid-sequence events into caller-owned `u32`
storage.  The sole generation identity is again one exact
`gpt-5.6-terra`/medium/default-service trajectory with an initial response and
at most three repairs; first correctness-green freezes immediately.

The deterministic gate has 84,041 cases.  Rust/oracle preflight, facts-on, and
facts-off each run every case at exact `src.len` capacity and at `src.len + 32`;
a subprocess boundary additionally requires every smaller capacity to trap
before writing.  The primary score is 30 fresh processes over a fixed 128 MiB
four-class corpus, with the same balanced ordering, paired ratios, stratified
bootstrap, and +/-2% verdict band as the first target.  The scope is explicitly
one-shot and synthetic-corpus-specific, not a claim about chunked streaming or
typical terminal text.

Prompt SHA-256 is
`81f023e583987d4610f15faa529b6481805dc4094fda2168146cf9ea9e9c903a`;
protocol SHA-256 is
`e786e949d1500c605ef37195dadc60e25380d4e02b7afc9f660d1cf5e062d960`.
Pre-freeze evidence: private reference candidate passed the full locked
evaluator (`correct cases=84041`); Rust/harness tests and Clippy are green;
strict C boundary and Python syntax checks are green; 16 MiB orchestrator smoke
completed all six non-scoring order blocks with identical counts/digests; root
`make check` and `make -C compiler check` are green.  No official model output,
proof report, IR, assembly, or timing result existed at this entry.

## D9a utf8parse score: default-floor win replicated (2026-07-13)

The first scoring attempt was invalidated at block 27 when the observed power
source changed from AC Power to Battery Power.  Its 28 completed raw rows and
all logs remain archived; none entered the result.  The protocol-authorized
full rerun binds that invalid campaign's metadata hash and the transition
reason, restarted at block 0 in a fresh append-free directory, and completed
all 30 processes and 90 samples under stable Battery Power with no recorded
power or thermal transition.

Median throughput in the valid campaign was 333.105 MiB/s Whitefoot facts-on,
319.673 MiB/s facts-off, and 280.474 MiB/s shipped Rust.  The preregistered
paired facts-on/Rust median ratio is 1.0980 with stratified bootstrap interval
[1.0849, 1.1448], a predeclared **meaningful Whitefoot win**.  Facts-on/facts-off
is 1.0051 with interval [0.9856, 1.0349], **inconclusive against the +/-2%
band** and unable to change the primary verdict.

Attribution remains negative for proof elision.  The facts-on and facts-off
reports are byte-identical, retain all 11 bounds sites, and prove none; their
optimized instruction bodies are also identical.  Rust's generic public
`Parser`/`Receiver` path monomorphizes and inlines into a call-free branch DFA,
so this result is not a dynamic-dispatch penalty either.  The defensible static
mechanism is different state numbering, control-flow layout, and source-loop
lowering for two implementations of the same DFA semantics; it does not imply
that expert Rust cannot choose a different layout.

This independently reproduces the default-floor win on a second shipped
library, with a much smaller effect than percent-decode.  D9a's requested
replication is therefore complete, but the claim remains limited to these two
first-green sources, frozen synthetic workloads, machine, and toolchain.  The
utf8parse corpus is deliberately equal-weight and malformed-heavy, and the
adapter is one-shot rather than a persistent streaming parser.  Canonical
evidence is in `experiments/default-floor/utf8parse/RESULTS.md`; valid raw
SHA-256 `71297ba0bfc2bc7b8af1f29b33f7c4769cb6c706f8a0c3f7c855363b86404ab3`,
analysis SHA-256
`1a16044495b3e4d2e41c6f49d6f32cf9390d95a3b40f5f3e8c278077e115ff1c`.

## D9a cross-target synthesis frozen; experiment expansion stops (2026-07-13)

The two separately preregistered target results now form the complete D9a
default-floor evidence set.  Report the target-specific paired throughput
ratios, never an average or pooled effect: percent-decode 1.6533 with
descriptive 95% bootstrap interval [1.6309, 1.6668], and one-shot utf8parse
1.0980 with interval [1.0849, 1.1448].  The targets were selected rather than
randomly sampled, the second was chosen after the first result, and both share
one model, compiler/checker, M4 host, and harness design.  This is cross-target
replication, not an ecosystem prevalence estimate or statistically independent
replication.

The supported claim is that, on these two frozen shipped-library tasks, the
first correctness-green `gpt-5.6-terra`/medium Whitefoot sources beat the released
crates' ordinary public paths through minimal safe adapters.  All 6 and 11
reported Whitefoot bounds sites respectively remained checked, so neither result
is a proof-elision win.  The evidence does not support “Whitefoot is generally
faster than Rust,” “AI Whitefoot is automatically optimal,” or any claim about the
expert-Rust ceiling.

Canonical wording, methodology, and caveats are frozen in
`experiments/default-floor/RESULTS.md`.  D9a's required second target is
satisfied; no third benchmark is needed for this gate.  Any later measurement
of either source is secondary sensitivity evidence and cannot replace its
primary campaign.  The experiment track now yields priority back to the wfc
self-hosting build track.

## OWN-1 index-atom flow omission recorded after mainline repair (2026-07-13)

E0.1 hostile review exposed a pre-existing mainline checker defect: an index
atom could read a field through an already-moved affine binding without entering
ownership flow.  Commit `38d642e` makes index atoms pass the normal
liveness/readability checks and adds the negative conformance case
`own1-neg-index-atom-after-move`.  This is an independent current-language bug
fix, not evidence for Flat records and not authorization for E0.1 production
semantics.

## GRAM-9 constructor drift and recursive projection drift repaired (2026-07-13)

Both executable frontends now enforce the selected strict three-address grammar:
a constructor is an expression and cannot occupy a call-argument or construction-
field atom position.  Auditing the pre-repair repository found 770 existing
violations: 745 in the 20 self-hosted compiler source files, 24 in 14 conformance
sources, and one embedded stage-0 fixture.  Of the compiler violations, 744
nullary Copy enum constructors are now bound once immediately before use; the
remaining violation was `AstConstructor()` inside the invalid constructor-as-atom
parser branch and disappeared with that branch.  The conformance migration
similarly binds 19 Copy values and binds then explicitly moves five affine
aggregate/payload values.  The self-hosted compiler pays 744 additional source
lines; this is measured maintenance evidence for any later GRAM-9 redesign, not
permission to ignore the current rule.  Existing performance and code-shape gates
remain authoritative for the generated program.

The same conformance pass repaired stage 0's recursive place suffix handling.
Its tokenizer deliberately retains dotted lower-case tokens, but the parser had
treated the suffix token in `index<T>(...).inner.value` as one field.  It now
expands every segment, while wfc's already-correct lexer/parser is pinned to two
successive field nodes.  Two negative GRAM-9 cases and one runnable recursive-
projection case make both boundaries durable.  These are current-language parser
repairs, not E0.1 record-storage semantics.

## Current-language expression-context ownership/type seams repaired (2026-07-13)

The E0.1 hostile review exposed a family of pre-existing checker seams after the
initial index liveness/readability repair at `38d642e`.  The complete repair keeps
the current language unchanged: projected places are classified by their projected
type; index atoms receive one ordinary ownership and type judgment; `index<T>`
checks its stated element type and exact u64 offset; and reference, box, and arena
holders require the explicit `deref(.)` spelling in index, match, try, and referent-
return contexts.

Match now consumes affine own scrutinees, copies tag-only scrutinees, rejects
explicit `move` of Copy or through a borrow, and requires an enum type.  Specialized
Result/Option/user-enum payload types enter flow; shared and exclusive borrowed
payload binders preserve ancestry and per-field aliasing, so derived access is legal,
siblings remain disjoint, and the parent holder remains frozen.  Contextual own
returns consume affine places without stealing through a borrow.  Try and const
bindings likewise retain concrete type metadata.  Conformance review also exposed
that the prototype type table had never encoded OP-6; it now implements the exact 29
total conversion pairs and returns `Result<Dst, NarrowError>` for every other
distinct numeric pair.

Twenty-five manifest/source gates cover the repaired seams: 19 negative diagnostics,
five runnable/accepted positives, and one checker-positive aggregate-payload case
that remains pending only because the disposable democ ABI cannot lower aggregate
enum payloads.  Two older fixtures were corrected: borrowed Copy payloads now use
explicit dereference while retaining byte-identical LLVM (SHA-256
`ab236e489742577015d080b06b6eb1a4d5d82c7486f5006da185e9f9df5ed`), and the
double-consumption negative now uses a genuinely affine payload rather than a
ratified Copy tag-only enum.

Hostile review found no remaining checker/conformance finding.  Verification is
94/94 checker units; 10,000 modelchecked programs with zero accepted soundness
violations; conformance 259 PASS / 14 SKIP / 90/90 rules; full `make check` ending
`ALL VERIFICATION LAYERS GREEN`; and clean whitespace checks.  This is an existing-
specification conformance repair, not E0.1 candidate semantics or authorization for
any record-storage design.

## E0.1 owner-review package revised; production design remains open (2026-07-13)

The owner-advisor review is durably dispositioned in
`experiments/data-layout-owning-sequence/REVIEW_RESPONSE.md`.  The exact rejected
prototype source is already archived at `68a55e4`; the initial index liveness repair
is narrowly attributed to `38d642e`; strict GRAM-9 and recursive projection are
repaired at `50a1ddd`; and the complete current-language expression-context checker
repair is `7438e17`.  Disposable executables remain outside the repository, while
every reviewed source artifact is recoverable.

The design recommendation is reopened.  Automatic structural Copy, declarative
`copy struct`, and nominally affine record storage are distinct ownership routes.
The OWN-1 tag-only precedent is answered on memory safety, nominal authority/private-
constructor invariants, and copy-cost visibility.  Recursive recipe, single-level
initializer, builder/initialized-prefix coupling, explicit Repeat/Clone, and Copy-
tier fill are preliminary alternatives with nonzero grammar/type/effect/lowering
prices; none is selected.  Non-builder E0.1a/E0.1b remains serial, while a builder
requires a newly approved coupled protocol.  An opaque kernel sequence would reverse
STOR-1 and therefore needs a full META-5 and design-tree redecision.  PATTERNS remains
a production gate, and float exclusion remains only a limitation of the archived
prototype.

No production specification, storage, wfc-layout, PATTERNS, teaching, or external-
model change is authorized.  The MCTS-Mem tree is unchanged while the owner choice
is open.  If a selected production route supersedes the recorded declarative-copy
path, the same decision must move that path to the appropriate `.alt/` branch with
paired reasons; selecting it instead must update its card with the deciding evidence.

`AFFINE_FIXED_BUILDER` screen.  The exact reviewed protocol SHA-256 is
`88d70083f9cf0219d558675b34a42f54c851793125fccebc07c3f48f4aa1b003`.
`OWNERSHIP_ROUTE_HOSTILE_REVIEW.md` records the three independent

The protocol compares complete initializer/ownership bundles, uses one direct
candidate contrast, makes `CURRENT` an unchanged-source identity control,
separates intrinsic route contradictions from invalid artifacts, freezes all
scored counts in Lock A, embargoes hidden writer results until campaign-wide

## General-purpose data-structure capability floor opened; E0.1 candidate work remains paused (2026-07-13)

The initialized-prefix discussion exposed an upstream process failure: E0.1's
fixed-record ownership screen had not first proved that ordinary checked Whitefoot
can express the dense, sparse, relocation, traversal, recursion, and stable-
identity transitions required by representative data structures.  The local
protocol was internally reviewed but its review scope did not include this
neighboring-operation census.  Under the standing owner instruction to stop
implementation and research first, the paired protocol remains paused before
Lock A.

`general-purpose-data-structure-capability-RESEARCH.md` establishes the
non-normative correction.  Its exact reviewed SHA-256 is
`48384d74624c40dad13514232985d39df6fa5910ba5bf513cd39f941440d82c7`.
The report separates protected baselines, mandatory floor contracts,
ordinary-library topology witnesses, held-out anti-special-casing witnesses,
and prevalence-gated options; maps each to a named canary; constrains R3 to
caller-observable contracts; freezes the workload/target and unique-winner
rules needed to interpret “fastest”; and records the finite copied-handle
impossibility boundary.  Public uninitialized payload access and standard-
library-only raw privilege remain rejected.  H-STORE must directly instantiate
the same checked storage transitions available to an unseen ordinary library.

`general-purpose-data-structure-capability-HOSTILE-REVIEW.md` (SHA-256
`b1d99a055372602aac0b8714661a09e9771e60ac66014f8a8ef2f34a625e9467`)
records three independent final `PASS` verdicts on the exact report bytes for
ownership/state/failure soundness, performance and R3 selection, and
specification/MCTS-Mem/process consistency.  Earlier rejected snapshots and
every blocking disposition are preserved in that review.

G0 is the only proposed next research step: freeze the role-mapped operation
registry, semantic contracts, payload/workload/target matrix, selection rule,
META-5 derivability ledger, held-out dependency budgets, and rejection
thresholds.  G0 itself needs review before candidate implementation.  No
language mechanism, collection representation, standard-library placement,
specification or PATTERNS change, wfc migration, scored run, external
disclosure, or default teaching is authorized.  The MCTS-Mem tree remains
unchanged because no production route was selected.

Sequential post-change verification passes: `make check` reports 90/90 rule
coverage, 10,000 model programs with zero accepted soundness violations, 259
conformance passes/14 skips, and `ALL VERIFICATION LAYERS GREEN`;
`make -C compiler check` also passes.

## D11 stages the data-structure capability floor by family; no next work is authorized (2026-07-13)

The owner confirmed Whitefoot's eventual general-purpose systems-language scope and
rejected the initial all-at-once G0 process. The durable ruling is D11 in
`optimizer-language-research/notes/user-directives.md`: a bounded G0-Core freezes
the global registry, coarse contracts, safety/no-tax laws, family dependencies,
exact held-out dependency budgets, reopening rules, and later-gate schemas. Each
family freezes exact semantics, algorithms, workloads, thresholds, soundness
fixtures, construction/tuning protocol, and META-5 derivability only in its own
Lock A immediately before candidate work. Candidate Freeze B remains a distinct
pre-scoring artifact freeze.

The current exact
`general-purpose-data-structure-capability-RESEARCH.md` SHA-256 is
`066c6e411cc0eefec608fb53371e4badfd91017617cefe63178ca101e19191b6`.
It separates family closure from the complete-floor claim: a family that passes
its assigned M/W/H obligations while protecting every B baseline may seek a
separate owner-approved production adoption, but no adoption may expose a public
transition, state topology, trusted fact, or trusted path outside the adopted
family locks. The complete claim waits for every protected B and every mandatory
M, topology W, and held-out H obligation. Append-only and recyclable stable
identity remain separate contracts, and the append-only path pays no generation
or recycling tax.

The first complete staged snapshot,
`3117ab458b0fc9a10f90a80dc8f923a5acfa2b7116bdbbcfc7b06b41a3323134`,
received no P0 finding but received three `REVISE` verdicts. Hostile review found
that candidate-construction effort was not preregistered, gating soundness
fixtures could change without reopening, W closure followed candidate claims,
cross-family safety followed claims rather than implemented/exposed state,
borrow-bearing payload scope was unstated, exact held-out budgets had weakened
to a schema, and stale E0.1 documents still exposed the superseded authorization
path. All findings were repaired. Three independent read-only scopes then
verified the final exact report bytes and returned `PASS` with no P0, P1, or P2
finding for ownership/state/failure soundness, performance/staging/selection,
and Constitution/specification/MCTS-Mem/repository consistency.

`general-purpose-data-structure-capability-HOSTILE-REVIEW.md` preserves the
initial exact review and records the D11 amendment, rejected hash, dispositions,
and final exact-hash passes; its SHA-256 is
`80cae6e2296da389581ed908b695cd0a301adfc399f5421adb8444e96b5b2265`.
The plan, compiler plan, experiment index, and E0.1 report, candidate, protocol,
review, and results surfaces now mark the old paired route as historical input.
G0-Core plus dense Family Lock A are necessary but not sufficient for a later
owner decision to lift the E0.1 pause; neither historical protocol restarts
automatically.

The MCTS-Mem root, pattern-doctrine, and data-model nodes gain sourced rationale
facts for the eventual general-purpose scope, ordinary-library completeness
test, family-by-family adoption boundary, and separate append-only/recyclable
contracts. No Item, Move, node, or `.alt/` path changes: the monolithic G0 was an
unratified research proposal, and no production mechanism, STOR-1 route, or

## D12 authorizes the complete G0-Core census and derivation research; mechanisms remain paused (2026-07-14)

The owner confirmed the general-purpose systems-language objective and
authorized completion of the research program proposed after D11. D12 records

finite completeness anchor; normalize observable contracts rather than copying
Rust mechanisms; derive a Pareto-small checked capability basis below named
containers; require ordinary no-unsafe library generativity, cross-ecosystem
witnesses, and explicit accounting for every deferred systems domain; and
preserve structural-performance and protected-baseline costs in the minimum.

The exact research charter is
`optimizer-language-research/implementation/minimal-systems-capability/G0-CORE-CHARTER.md`,

`11b017da99da40713038bcbdcdeee0787e31a258b50e9c5dbc0b5ad52edfcc13`.

`2d8144b7880597b6e6d3dfd63a9a9efae3f533d3`; freezes inventory,
normalization, derivation, performance-control, review, and completion schemas;
and names the detailed first closure as the sequential, unique-owner,
ordinary-library data-structure floor. The complete systems envelope remains
accounted but not silently claimed by that closure.

This authorization covers source inspection, reproducible census tooling,

## G0-Core closes the pre-review obligation, route, iteration, and witness accounting (2026-07-14)

The D12-authorized synthesis now separates 49 operational obligations, 12
orthogonal proof dimensions, and 16 global laws without selecting one language
primitive per obligation. `BR-STORED` preserves the missing lifetime/provenance
question for borrow-bearing payloads; the first detailed floor remains
explicitly region-free and borrow-free. `IT-COMPOSE` and W-PIPE require reusable
zero-materialization traversal rather than a hand-fused loop. `F-MMIO` preserves
the checked volatile/device-memory need while keeping raw-pointer volatile
spelling inadmissible.

The classifier now has independent surface-evidence and underlying-need axes.
Across all 5,369 canonical stable declarations it records 4,609 safe contract
anchors, 170 safe boundaries, 273 unsafe boundaries, and 317 Rust-only surfaces;
the underlying routes are 1,033 G0 contracts, 302 library contracts, 3,765
later-family contracts, seven exact frame services, 43 redundant declarations,
217 declarations with no independent need, and two true non-goals. The only
true non-goals are `catch_unwind` and `resume_unwind` under EFF-4. Raw, unsafe,
manual-lifetime, leak, partial-initialization, FFI, atomic, pin, and MMIO evidence
retains a named safe displacement instead of being mislabeled as a non-goal.

The detailed census contains 258 normalized rows. A new exact D10 crosswalk
routes all 150 stable iteration/range declarations once (132 iteration, 18
range; 107 contract routes, 43 redundant surfaces), keeps `ExactSize` and
`Fused` separate, and splits the stable range surface into 13 contracts. The
258-row derivation matrix records E=4, P=0, U=10, X=212, FRAME=4, DEFERRED=19,
BOUNDARY=9, and NG=0. BOUNDARY means the Rust spelling is inadmissible while
the checked need remains live; it is not a non-goal.

Visible and held-out witness budgets now use exact closed allowlists. W-POOL
freezes generation exhaustion, retirement, memory history, cross-pool policy,
and returned-borrow ownership. W-ARENA promises owner-tied borrows across later
allocations without importing physical address stability, rejects reset while
borrows live, and prices chunk allocation. H-STORE includes dependent-state and
result-reborrow obligations and receives only the public allocator facade.
H-LRU and H-IPQ freeze exact affine outcomes; H-IPQ must implement heap repair
over selected dense/map public APIs rather than import a finished heap.

Focused verification passes: deterministic classifier regeneration, exact Rust
census, 258-row data-contract verification, 150-row D10 verification, 258-row
derivation verification against all 49 capability IDs, exact witness-ID checks,

## D14-R1 closes the privileged-gate synthesis for owner review (2026-07-15)

The hostile-reviewed research selects one admission-gate direction and rejects
premature public-basis closure. The direction is a sealed capability admission
verifier with a compiler-embedded base root and one authenticated signed
approval-snapshot predicate for scoped out-of-band capsules. Ordinary source
has no privilege-admission spelling or flag. Proof over existing public checked
semantics remains an ordinary artifact available to every producer; only a new
machine, helper, lowering, backend, ABI, OS, device, or foreign semantic edge
requires a capsule. Every proposition consumed for safety, resource authority,
or optimizer facts must come from static proof, runtime
validation/enforcement, or explicit ledgered trust; ordinary abstract
container correctness is outside that obligation unless promoted to a checked
contract or fact.

The bounded sequential candidate now has nine schematic roles over full,
prefix, interval, and two-range shapes, including shape-preserving swap and
replace. It remains blocked on opaque generative sealing, full/inline adoption,
focus, cleanup, allocation policy, arbitrary relocation, exact static rules,
and protected-path evidence. H-STORE's dense-prefix route establishes payload
safety through checked indexing, so its abstract key/position invariant does
not justify a general proof logic; the frozen `ST-SPARSE` requirement is
recorded for re-adjudication as a possible mechanism overconstraint. The
26-domain companion is an admission/dependency map, not a derivability proof.

Two independent exact-byte hostile reviews report no remaining P0 or P1
finding. The reviewed report, witness derivations, admission map, and review
hashes are respectively
`3f1998623e2278585867f512a20da2d9c218b1b0a114f26b28932a655254acf8`,
`fd334c57d76f064d69d2bd9c6f114c94ff6caad6fbd666c76bf98947de2d3deb`,
`ebab8f2e0592d9524d0fd7db7382d961b60b52bab5e9e519a797b19606cdf4bd`,
and `72fb432f1db15b97faa400592a4fc83c1f86fd121b312bd11e6e70b989b17a92`.

The requested next research is staged: Gate Authentication Lock A and Bounded
Sequential Safety Kernel Lock B only. A general-predicate lock opens only after
a formal counterexample or later separately authorized measurement proves it
necessary; shared and concurrent families remain later. This step selects no
public basis, language or specification rule, compiler feature, standard
library, container, experiment, fact channel, or production action. Stages A
and B, every implementation, and every execution require explicit owner
authorization.

D16-R3 (2026-07-16): the spec-mass measurement returned FAIL against its preregistered bands. Real normative text was authored for three sealed forms (seq 24 rows / 2,947 tokens, table 18 rows / 2,774, conc_queue 11 rows / 2,395, shared conventions 1,078 — measured with tiktoken cl100k_base) and two full cards (LRU 3,014, FIFO/ring 2,152); extrapolation over the re-cut catalog gives ~65.5k tokens central (~58-71k range) against the <=40k PASS and >55k FAIL lines. Cards are ~56% of the total; kernel deltas cost separately ~10-13k at the measured ~169 tokens/rule, so the combined new normative mass (~75-78k) is ~5x the existing 90-rule kernel (15.2k). Per the preregistered protocol, reduction precedes any implementation. Five concrete levers identified: (1) move card example code to the teaching corpus — biggest single swing (~-15k), requires an explicit owner ruling on whether card code counts against the spec budget; (2) cards cite op rows by rule ID instead of re-quoting (~-4-6k, also removes a normative-fork drift hazard); (3) default-elision row format (~-3-4k); (4) shared failure/fact clause macros plus card prose trim (~-6-7k); (5) marginal row drops (~-1-1.5k). Levers 2-5 need no owner ruling and are being validated by re-authoring the measured samples under the reduced conventions. Authored drafts preserved in `systems-performance-coverage/m2-spec-mass/`; count evidence in `evidence/m2-spec-mass-count.json`. No production change authorized.

D16-R4 (2026-07-16): reduction levers validated by full lossless rewrite and recount (cl100k_base; automated audit confirms every trap string, rule ID, op name, and codegen mark survives). Results against the bands: original projection 66,578 FAIL; levers 2-4 with cards keeping code 59,862 still FAIL; plus card-code-to-teaching-corpus 52,735 REDUCE; PASS (<=40k) is ~13k out of reach of encoding levers alone. Structural findings: the default-elision/macro conventions add a fixed +732 tokens to S.0 that amortizes only across the full catalog (per-form op-content ratio 0.899); card savings are mix-sensitive under code-kept (LRU-like 0.804 vs FIFO-like 0.978) but robust under code-relocated (0.647/0.735). Consequence: reaching PASS requires a structural boundary decision, not more encoding — the candidate mechanism follows the repository's own precedent (kernel spec and PATTERNS.md are already separate documents): the always-in-context surface = kernel deltas + sealed/library interface appendix + per-card contract stubs (~11k + ~30k), with full cards in an on-demand teaching layer (~1.7k each). Whether that tiered-context model satisfies D2 is an explicit owner decision queued for morning review. Reduced artifacts in `systems-performance-coverage/m2-spec-mass/reduced-*.md`; recount evidence in `evidence/m2-reduction-recount.json`. No production change authorized.

D16-R7 (2026-07-16): io-file is now an explicit 17-row enumeration in `systems-performance-coverage/IO-ROW-ENUMERATION.md`, replacing the load-bearing phrase "plus what wal needs" with a closed set (the only wal need missing from the re-cut list was ftruncate; the four fs-namespace rows are the seam the member-audit FATAL exposed). The Darwin durability pin is recorded: fdatasync/fsync/dir-fsync rows MUST lower to fcntl(F_FULLFSYNC) on macOS — plain Darwin fsync returns before the drive cache is stable and F_BARRIERFSYNC is ordering-only — and until the lowering is pinned no macOS WAL-durability test counts as evidence. Three genuinely non-unifiable contracts flagged rather than papered over: O_DIRECT (macOS F_NOCACHE is a weaker advisory; contract promises only the intersection), the durability rows (unifiable only via the F_FULLFSYNC pin), and the block-size query (per-platform syscalls; 4Kn/512e correctness is a battery item). The UDP rows are amended from conditional-KEEP to DEFER on honest scenario-pinning failure: the only UDP-naming numbered scenario's par targets are all TCP, single-datagram blocking rows are not the batching sub-shape it names, and every nameable UDP consumer is either non-numbered or rides already-deferred capabilities; reinstatement triggers recorded (dns_resolve firing via the UDP stub-resolver route, or admission of a numbered UDP par scenario). TCP rows stay kept. No production change authorized.

D16-R8 (2026-07-16): two executable micro-verifications corrected audit assumptions (Apple M4/macOS, indicative constants; sources and numbers in `systems-performance-coverage/evidence/microbench/`). (a) The sealed-table clone constant for POD entries measures ~1-2 ns/entry (std 1.03, hashbrown 2.06 at 1M u64->u64; bandwidth-bound bulk copy) against the audited assumption of ~50-100 ns/entry — wrong by ~25-100x, which strengthens the COW-republish card's publish cost for scalar tables while owning-value tables remain unmeasured and need their own number before the read-mostly falsifier applies to them. (b) macOS accept() does not honor listener SO_RCVTIMEO (blocks indefinitely; setsockopt succeeds silently), so the member audit's timed-accept graceful-drain mechanism is broken on Darwin; per-connection SO_RCVTIMEO deadlines work as documented. The self-connect-wakeup or kqueue-based drain fallback is now the required Darwin path, the acceptance battery must exercise it, and the Linux timed-accept claim must be verified on the deployment target before ratification. No production change authorized.

D16-R9 (2026-07-16): owning-value clone constants measured, completing the two-regime flag (numbers and sources in `systems-performance-coverage/evidence/microbench/`). The clone constant spans >1000x by value kind: POD ~1-2 ns/entry, 24B-string ~10-30, 200B ~36-250 (scale-sensitive), 4KB-buffer ~360-3060 ns/entry (page-fault/bandwidth regime). The prior ~50-100 ns/entry assumption is correct only for ~200B values near 1M entries. Recorded with an interpretive correction to the measuring agent's summary: since COW-republish's publish cost IS the clone cost, the pattern is viable for POD/handle tables (~1-2 ms per 1M-entry publish) and non-viable for KB-value tables except at very low update rates — that regime belongs to the sharded-mutex card or the deferred in-place concurrent table. The read-mostly card's falsifier must select its constant by the target scenario's value type. No production change authorized.

D16-R12 (2026-07-16): independent hostile review of the 15 loan/freeze rules ran with executable counterexamples (three lenses, 583 programs run; raw output in `evidence/m1-hostile-review.json`) and REOPENS the loan-judgment gate. Soundness lens: one FATAL — R14 as written lacks a pairwise cross-slot disjointness clause, so a par statement passing overlapping split-unique and replicate-shared views of the same place is machine-ACCEPTED (four aliasing variants confirmed; a spec-level hole, not merely implementation); one MAJOR — mint legality never consults the source parameter's own borrow mode, so a helper taking a shared reference can unique-mint it internally and launder mutation under a caller's live cursor (an unstated dependency on the base ownership layer; standalone M1 accepts it). Fidelity lens: the 48/48 headline is real (no hardcoded outcomes, faithful transcriptions, mutation testing confirms core semantics are pinned) but five machine-proven implementation divergences all err toward accept (confined sources droppable under live loans; own-mode confined args to clause-none ops never consumed; R11 gate keyed on AST annotation; R12 liveness/holder-name clauses and R5 preconditions corpus-dead; R13 unimplemented) and R9 as frozen cannot type the checker's own form table without an undocumented carve-out. Expressiveness lens: SURVIVES — all six catalog idioms machine-ACCEPT in writer-natural shapes (17 blessed probes accept, 8 boundary probes reject as predicted), so the entry/rebalance/cursor/try-lock/sharded-map/buffered-read answers stand; plus one extra same-statement aliased-mint flag routed to the soundness repair. Every finding carries a named local fix from its reviewer; none identifies an architectural blocker. Per the standing repair rule, the M1 PASS is suspended until the repairs land, the corpus absorbs every review program as frozen expectations, and the full machine check reruns green. No production change authorized.

D16-R15 (2026-07-16): the kernel-shape parity dry run validates the sealed-kernel implementation shapes (Apple M4/NEON, indicative; artifacts and RESULTS.md in `systems-performance-coverage/m3a-kernel-dryrun/`). C implementations of the catalog's exact seq and table shapes versus Rust Vec and hashbrown 0.17.1+foldhash: push-then-sum 0.67x (beats Vec), build 1.18x, hit-lookup 1.07x, iterate-sum 0.71x (beats hashbrown iter), miss-lookup 1.26x at the band edge with the probe shape confirmed in disassembly (one 16-byte control load + compare + mask per group, empty-check reusing the same vector) and the residual attributed to the hasher approximation. Correctness leg: three seeds of one million mixed operations against a std HashMap oracle with per-op comparison — zero divergence, exercising in-place rehash purge, 2x growth, tombstone reuse. Four catalog findings recorded: (1) SUBSTANTIVE — S.2 must pin the array-of-structs (K,V) slot layout: struct-of-arrays doubled steady-state insert cache misses to ~2.0x; (2) the guaranteed-inline codegen contract for push is load-bearing (1.6x without register promotion across the hot loop; LTO used as its stand-in); (3) the probe contract must state the fused single group load (separate helper loads violate the pin); (4) iteration parity requires group-scanning control bytes (per-bucket branching is ~2x). No production change authorized.

D16-R17 (2026-07-16): the SPSC queue dry run passes all three legs (artifacts and RESULTS.md in `systems-performance-coverage/m6a-spsc-dryrun/`; model check independently rerun before recording). Exhaustive small-bound model check of the catalog's protocol under a release/acquire operational semantics: 249 reachable states, SAFE (no lost/duplicated/wrong item, no read-before-published slot, FIFO, termination); the mutation leg weakens each of the four acquire/release halves to relaxed one at a time and every weakening produces a machine-found violation at this bound — including the proof that the head-side pair is a pure ordering fence, invisible on strong memory models and required on ARM. Benchmarks vs rtrb 0.3.4 (Apple M4, indicative): batched-32 throughput ~1050M items/s (band >=80M — 13x over); round-trip latency ~31 ns/way misses the 6-15 ns band, but the band is calibrated for pinned x86 servers — rtrb itself measures ~39 ns/way on this machine and our kernel BEATS it, so the miss is platform floor, not implementation; re-measure on the deployment target before any claim. Correctness: 50M items strict FIFO. The zero-RMW WIN claim is confirmed at the instruction level: hot send/recv paths contain zero read-modify-write atomics (no ldadd/ldaxr/stlxr/cas/swp), and the amortized fast path has no atomic acquire at all thanks to cursor caching. No catalog deviation was needed; cache-line separation of cursors recorded as standard practice, measured non-load-bearing at batch-32. No production change authorized.

D18-R5 (2026-07-17): BRAND-1 (brand-cross-fn) is drafted as DELTA 5 in `m2-spec-mass/KERNEL-DELTAS-DRAFT.md`. Structure: brands reuse the R9/R10 signature-tie machinery verbatim (tie totality, callee seeding, return propagation, transfer on move), with exactly one generalization — R10(a) compares brand IDENTITIES rather than places, where an identity is a lexical place (arena ids: verbatim place comparison) or a generative skolem (queue brands: CQ-2's fresh-per-execution identity, which place comparison would wrongly collapse for loop-minted queues). Adoption order updated: BRAND-1 before the concurrency delta; mint-and-return waits on the BRAND-MINT binder. D18-R20 (2026-07-17): the concurrency delta full hostile review returns NOT ADOPTABLE / BLOCK / REJECT — all three independent reviewers converge on the same structural verdict with concrete data-race programs (evidence in `evidence/conc-review.json`). Three FATAL classes, each an accepted two-thread unsynchronized access: (1) spawn-capture loans reuse R14/AMD-1 statement-local machinery whose soundness premise is that the par statement lasts as long as the bodies — false for spawn, whose statement returns immediately while the child runs, so capture loans evaporate at statement end and the parent (or a second spawn) freely touches a place a live child holds; fix is persistent per-capture loan entries held to the join, which is genuinely new disjointness machinery (the "no new dataflow" claim is withdrawn). (2) The ordinary-value Shareable predicate ("deeply immutable / no interior &uniq reachable") is vacuously true for every spellable container and never consults payload Shareability, so a post-AMD-6 endpoint stored in a seq is reached by two threads running the &-receiver clone op; fix is a total structural induction "Shareable iff every field/payload Shareable" with an explicit fail-closed default and reconciliation of the cq_tx_clone/cq_rx_clone rows (they take &-receivers, contradicting CQ-3's "every endpoint op takes &uniq"). (3) The guard's &uniq interior view carries no loan entry tying it to the guard, so a self-tied helper returns it past the unlock — two live &uniq to one location, a lock-free write racing a locked write. The deepest finding, spanning reviewers: the kernel defines no happens-before memory model, so D1 race-freedom is asserted rather than checkable for these forms, and R15 as written is a per-invocation predicate that cannot carry mutex mutual exclusion — a name for an unstated proof. Verdict architecture note: the SHAPE is right (static capabilities off AMD-6 classes, a closed set of sealed sync points, trap=abort) and every direct brand/identity forgery was repelled; the failure is that the delta was drafted on top of a memory model that does not exist. Honest rule count ~11 not 4. This delta requires a memory-model foundation before its three mechanisms can be rebuilt — materially heavier than the other five deltas, which are review-clean. Redraft dispatched with a memory-model-first ordering. No production change authorized.

Cross-references verified to resolve. This authorizes nothing; it is the deliberation input for the five decisions in D18-R21..R25. No production change authorized.

D18-R27 (2026-07-17): preregistered ladder rung M8 (checked-source SIMD memchr) passes as a dry run, confirming a catalog placement without needing an owner decision (artifacts in `systems-performance-coverage/m8-memchr-dryrun/`). The load-bearing result is the assembly: the DOM-1(b) len-check-domination bound (Delta 4, review-clean) discharges every main-loop bounds check so the bounds-modeled NEON memchr compiles to a byte-identical 64B/step inner loop as the unchecked reference — zero residual compare/branch per step. Bulk throughput vs the memchr crate (2.8.3; the caret 2.7 resolved to current 2.x, same SIMD mechanism) is at par: 16KB 0.99-1.00x, 1MB 0.93-1.01x, bounds-modeled within 1.02x of unchecked everywhere; a non-discharged opaque bound costs ~1.7-1.87x on bulk, which is exactly what the fact saves. Differential correctness over 1M random cases: zero divergence across rust/unchecked/modeled/naive. One marginal miss (16B-needle-at-25% short latency ~2.13x vs the 2.0x band) is the reference's small-input path, not checking (b/a is 1.00 there). Consequence: memchr STAYS a checked library over the machine-core SIMD primitive; no sealed kernel warranted. Honest scope: this exercises DOM-1(b) len-check domination on a fixed-length slice (the measured easy case); it does not test the harder variable-offset/F3-class facts (SQLite cell walks, TLV) the catalog gates separately. No production change authorized.

D18-R28 (2026-07-17): preregistered ladder rung M4 (arena branded-id deref) passes as a dry run (artifacts in `systems-performance-coverage/m4-arena-dryrun/`; dossier §2.4 wording corrected accordingly). Assembly confirms the check-free path: the branded-id deref is a bare scaled-index load (`add x9,x8,x9,lsl #4` then loads, no compare/branch) — BRAND-1's affine-id design removes both the which-arena and the generation check. The always-on-elidable checked fallback adds exactly two data-dependent instructions per deref (cmp + trap-branch, uneliminable in a pointer chase) but costs ~0% (b/a 0.96-1.03x at every residency) because the traversal is latency-bound and the compare hides under the next-node load-use latency — far inside the 1.25x bar. Honest correction the run forced: vs a RAW-pointer C arena, index-based deref is ~1.63x at L1-resident (the base+idx*16 address arithmetic, a large fraction of ~0.9ns L1 latency) and at par (~1.0-1.05x) only at L2/DRAM residency; this index-vs-pointer gap is orthogonal to checking (the check-free path pays it too) and an index-based C arena matches it, so the dossier's "at par with C" is softened to "at par for memory-resident walks; ~1.6x a raw-pointer arena for L1 hot walks (index arithmetic, not checking)." Cross-cut with M8: data-dependent checks hide in latency-bound chases, loop-induction checks are DOM-1-discharged to nothing — the safety check is cheap either way; brands' value is removing the which-arena/generation checks, asm-confirmed. Differential correctness identical across all three variants at every size. No production change authorized.

GOV-1 (2026-07-18): added an owner-gated guard for the kernel spec and the semantics-bearing test surface, after the parked `parked_edits`/D20-R3 branch edited `kernel-spec-v0.6.md` in place and rewrote `test_checker.py` without owner approval (that branch stays parked; main is unchanged by it). `make check` gains a `spec-guard` layer (`tools/spec_guard.py` + `tools/test_spec_guard.py`, 13 regressions) that hash-pins the 7 numbered specs, 288 conformance expected verdicts, 3 frozen oracle digests, and 115 reference-test functions against an approved baseline (`governance/guard-baseline.json`) chained to a logged owner approval (`governance/APPROVALS.md`). A guarded change with no matching logged approval fails the build; adding new tests or conformance cases stays free; numbered specs must bump version + rename (in-place edits fail outright). `CLAUDE.md`/`AGENTS.md` gain three byte-identical standing rules for the ask-owner -> log-approval -> commit protocol, and a `make approve-spec REASON=...` target records an approval after the owner grants it. Enforcement is process + audit trail, not cryptographic: the owner approves in session and the approval is logged for audit. Verified end-to-end on the real tree: an in-place v0.6 edit and a reference-test rewrite both turn spec-guard red; a new conformance case stays green. `make check` and `make -C compiler check` are green.

GOV-2 (2026-07-18): recorded the no-reborrow question in the plan as an OPEN investigation, not a relaxation, and strengthened the spec-updating rule to require evidence. Finding (from main's wfc source, not the parked branch): wfc reborrows at ~1,279 sites (e.g. `frontend_unit_reset` forms `&uniq 'frontend_reset_tokens deref(analyzed).tokens`), which v0.6 (PATTERNS P4 / T-A) forbids; the ban keeps the ownership no-alias facts unconditional. Owner ruling: wfc is early code and NOT a source of truth, so the choice — keep the rule and rewrite the code, or change the rule — must be decided by recorded pros/cons, a no-alias/T-A soundness argument, and measured data before any owner-gated spec change; do not relax the rule to make wfc pass. THE-PLAN Phase 2 gains an open-decision gate binding that resolution before the whole-unit lowering / facts-off self-hosting fixpoint (no function may remain unsupported at Phase 2 exit). CLAUDE.md/AGENTS.md gain a standing rule: the accepted spec is the authority, the current wfc source is not; a spec change is earned by a soundness or design argument that stands on its own, never by existing code. governance/APPROVALS.md now requires a rule-relaxation or semantic approval to cite where its investigation is recorded. Wording was adversarially reviewed (three lenses + synthesis) before landing, which caught an open-ended 'unsupported' parking that contradicted the fixpoint gate, a dangling OBL-4 reference (present only on parked_edits), and an approval loophole. `make check` and `make -C compiler check` green.

REBORROW-INV (2026-07-18): ran the recorded no-reborrow investigation (THE-PLAN Phase 2 gate) as a read-only multi-agent study; dossier at `optimizer-language-research/implementation/reborrow-investigation/DOSSIER.md`. Verified all wfc reborrows are transient, statement-scoped, non-escaping call arguments through `&uniq` parameters (989 uniq + 73 shared; zero bound/returned/stored/given). Option A (keep the rule, rewrite wfc): the 'acceptable cost' claim BROKE on the recursive analyzer core (`semantic_body_analyze_atom` family returns a value AND holds two `&uniq` borrows; the only reborrow-free encoding is an FN-7 opaque owned mega-context or STOR-1-blocked take/replace) — ~979/989 sites rewrite cleanly, the ~10 hottest do not. Option B (relax to bounded reborrow): survived a soundness kill-shot attempt — 20 programs driven through the parked-branch checker found no aliasing; the closest approach (sequential analog of the D18-R20..R24 guard FATAL) was caught by the OWN-4 region tie — but rests on the still-open OBL-4 formal obligation and an un-run noalias fact-channel re-audit. Recommendation: neither pure option is clean; pursue the NARROWEST relaxation covering 100% of wfc (OWN-6 statement-scoped suspension of an unbound call-argument child only, deferring OWN-14 result-transfer/downgrade), gated on discharging OBL-4 for that fragment (widened model check + FR reconciliation + pinned census) and the CLAUDE.md-mandated hostile fact-channel review of the noalias derivation under lineage. Not driven by 'wfc uses reborrows'; wfc usage is treated as a cost signal for Option A. No spec/code/test change; owner decides direction.

REBORROW-DIR (2026-07-18): owner ruled to pursue the narrow bounded-reborrow relaxation ("let's move with this direction, relax to allow bounded reborrow"). This authorizes the VERIFICATION PROGRAM toward an owner-gated kernel-spec change: the minimal-rule design (`reborrow-investigation/MINIMAL-RULE.md`), the widened model-check that discharges OBL-4 for the admitted fragment, the Featherweight-Rust reconciliation, and the hostile no-alias fact-channel review. It is NOT approval to edit the kernel spec: per the standing rule, the exact v0.6->v0.7 delta requires the completed evidence packet plus a separate explicit owner approval logged in `governance/APPROVALS.md`; approval of a direction is never approval to edit the spec. The minimal rule admits only OWN-6 statement-scoped suspension of an unbound call-argument child (covering 100% of wfc's 989 uniq + 73 shared sites); OWN-14 result-transfer/downgrade and bound/returned children are deferred with recorded re-entry triggers. Owner confirmed performance is not expected to regress: the noalias fact is preserved (authority moves down the ownership tree, never forks), which the fact-channel review must confirm. REBORROW-RULE-R2 (2026-07-18): the draft minimal reborrow rule was adversarially reviewed (three lenses: soundness/coverage/decidability) and found BROKEN — a concrete miscompile. v0.6 permits borrow-returning functions, so a callee could launder the statement-scoped child's loan into a bound result outliving the statement, giving two usable `&uniq` to one place (F001 break, not just a lost optimization). Rev 2 fixes it by requiring the receiving call to return a non-borrow (`own`/`unit`) — closing the launder WITHOUT re-adding the deferred OWN-14, and verified to keep 100% wfc coverage (every wfc callee returns `own`). Also fixed: an index-sibling gloss contradicting OWN-7, `'c`-confinement enforcement (locally-introduced region, not caller-supplied, not outliving the statement), the OWN-5 carve-in/carve-out wording, the OWN-12 effect-row ancestor exemption, and the eligible-holder restriction (parameter/let holders only, no match binders). Coverage 100% (1,062 sites), decidable, direction viable. Rule at `reborrow-investigation/MINIMAL-RULE.md` rev 2. Next: the widened model-check that generates borrow-returning callees + caller-supplied/multi-statement `'c` and asserts no two live overlapping `uniq` unless one derives from the other. No spec/code/test change.

REBORROW-MODELCHECK (2026-07-18): built and ran the widened model-check for the minimal reborrow rule (rev 2), discharging OBL-4 item 1 for the admitted fragment at the model level. Harness `reborrow-investigation/modelcheck/modelcheck_reborrow.py`: generates random programs including the two escape vectors the review surfaced (borrow-returning callees, caller-supplied/multi-statement `'c`), runs the minimal-rule checker, and runs an INDEPENDENT operational oracle (exclusivity ground truth) on every accepted program. The oracle is proven non-vacuous: it catches the launder aliasing when a deliberately-broken rev-1 checker accepts it. Result over 1,000,000 programs (deterministic seed): 0 soundness violations on accepted; 363,153/363,153 launder attempts rejected (100%, all at OWN-6 rmode-non-borrow); 9/9 self-tests pass. Over-rejection (307,205 rejected-but-oracle-clean) is conservative and fail-closed and does not affect wfc's always-accepted shape. Honest scope: a focused abstract model of the reborrow rule, not the production full-language checker; folding the rule into `prototype/checker` and extending the shared oracle with exclusivity is post-spec production work. Remaining evidence for the packet: Featherweight-Rust reconciliation + hostile no-alias fact-channel review. No spec/code/test change.

REBORROW-FACTCHANNEL (2026-07-18): completed the FR reconciliation + hostile no-alias fact-channel review of the minimal reborrow rule. Verdict PASS-WITH-CONDITIONS: all three attack lenses returned noalias unbroken (no reachable miscompile in v0.6; performance preserved); FR reconciliation HOLDS — the rule is Featherweight Rust's `*w` reborrow restricted to singleton lineages, the checker stays singleton-rooted, and the lexical statement-scoped suspend is stricter-sound (a subset of FR's flow prohibition). The review CORRECTED rev 2's plan: it surfaced the own-wrapped launder (a callee returning `own Wrapper` that stashes the child borrow in a field — legal under §1.2's top-level-mode-only check, impossible today only because v0.6 storage is grammatically borrow-free but UN-numbered), and requires the exclusivity assertion to ship UNCONDITIONALLY (no derived_from carve-out) with a lineage-aware alias-scope emitter. Binding conditions A-F recorded. Evidence packet at `reborrow-investigation/PACKET.md` assembles all four legs (coverage 100%/1,062 sites; model-check 1M programs/0 violations; FR reconciliation; fact-channel PASS-WITH-CONDITIONS) and the exact v0.6->v0.7 delta — now including ONE new numbered rule (borrow-free/region-free storage), correcting rev 2's 'no new numbered rule'. Awaiting owner approval of the exact delta before any spec change. No spec/code/test change.

REBORROW-V07-LANDED (2026-07-18): landed the owner-approved bounded-reborrow relaxation as `spec/kernel-spec-v0.7.md`. READER-PROFILE-ADMIT (2026-07-18): admitted the first acyclic-decision ("reader") body-semantics profile in wfc, moving `lexer_scan_op_suffix` and `lexer_scan_word` from legal-but-unsupported to clean — the execution cursor's next Phase-2 step after region retention. New `compiler/src/semantic_reader.wf` (21 functions), dispatched between the scanner-block and linear gates as `SemanticCapabilityAcyclic` (last enum variant); `llvm_supported.wf` marks it not-lowered (this slice adds no LLVM lowering, per the cursor). The design is fail-closed: default Unsupported; an exhaustive signature gate (source borrow + two `own u64` params + `own u64` return + `reads('s), traps`) that admits exactly the two targets and excludes the Bool-returning `lexer_ampuniq_at`; all-paths-return flow over nested `let`/`match`/early-return (a `match` Returns only when both arms Return; no dead code after a return; empty/falling blocks rejected); arm-local binding scope save/restore; primitive expression typing; named multi-argument user calls with arg count/order/type/mode matching; and region-argument + effect containment. Unit is now 510 functions / 17 clean / 493 unsupported / 0 rejected; self-parse deterministic at 1,237,377 bytes / 244,886 tokens / 122,594 unique-head nodes; the source-order frontier moves to `lexer_ampuniq_at` as predicted. FACT-CHANNEL REVIEW (a body-semantics profile lets the optimizer assume more, so a hostile review ran BEFORE merge, not on a green gate): a three-lens adversarial pass (type-confusion, control-flow, call/region/effect) found ONE false-clean — the equality branch set `operation_ok = True()` unconditionally, admitting the ill-typed `ieq<Bool>`/`ine<Bool>` (OP-1 defines `ieq ine ilt ile igt ige` over integer T only; the Bool domain has only `band bor bxor bnot`, with no equality op). Fixed by pinning the equality operand to a scalar (`operation_ok = operand_scalar`, mirroring the already-sound ordered-comparison branch). Added non-vacuous regression `assert_reader_bool_equality_rejected` in test_semantic_unit.py (ieq/ine<Bool> -> Unsupported; structurally-identical band<Bool> and integer ieq/ine<u64> -> clean), verified failing on the pre-fix code and passing on the fixed. A focused re-attack on the fixed analyzer confirmed the fix closes the hole with zero over-rejection and no sibling operand-domain hole: the arithmetic/ordered/logical branches all fail-closed; `bxor` has no recognizer (-> Unsupported); `bnot` is unary and fails the 3-child shape gate before any operator branch. `make check` (ALL LAYERS GREEN) and `make -C compiler check` green on main after removing the merged scratch worktree (project-state counts one roadmap and had seen the gitignored worktree copy of THE-PLAN.md; os.walk does not respect gitignore). RECORDED RESIDUALS (sound for classification now; close before widening or lowering, none blocking this no-lowering, single-buffer/single-region slice): (1) a callee buffer parameter's mode-region is not tied to the callee's region parameter (asymmetric with the reader's own signature check) — fix before admitting multiple buffers/regions, buffer lets, or buffer/reference returns; (2) the callee scan accepts multiple `reads` effects, only the last region-checked; (3) the arithmetic branch collapses op identity/effect (iadd.trap vs isub.wrap) into "arithmetic -> u64" and stays sound only because the recognizers are pinned to the T-returning modes — carry op identity/effect through when lowering is added, and flag any broadening to a Result-returning `.checked` mode; (4) CLEAN is trust-only until this profile gains downstream codegen re-verification. Non-guarded surfaces only (semantic_reader.wf, test_semantic_unit.py, THE-PLAN cursor); no spec/conformance/oracle change and no owner approval required.

READER-PROFILE-BOOL-RETURN (2026-07-18): extended the acyclic-decision reader profile to admit `own Bool`-returning acyclic functions alongside `own u64`, admitting `lexer_ampuniq_at` (unit now 510 / 18 clean / 492 unsupported / 0 rejected; self-parse 1,242,113 bytes / 245,780 tokens / 123,022 nodes; frontier moves to `lexer_scan_string`). Three additions in `compiler/src/semantic_reader.wf`: (1) the signature return gate accepts u64 OR Bool (u8 still rejected), and `semantic_reader_run` threads the actual declared return type (child ordinal 6) into `analyze_block`/`analyze_return` instead of a hardcoded u64; (2) a unary `bnot` path in `analyze_table_call` (exactly 2 children, Bool type-arg, Bool operand -> Bool result), the only unary op, gated ahead of the 3-child binary path; (3) an `AstConstructor` branch in `analyze_expr` typing nullary `True()`/`False()` as Bool via `semantic_prelude_constructor_code`, every other constructor Unsupported. Still no LLVM lowering. FACT-CHANNEL REVIEW: a hostile review of the three new paths returned GO / no false-clean. Constructor typing is sound because `True`/`False` are reserved — spec TYPE-6 mandates global enum-variant-name uniqueness and PRE-1 declares `enum Bool { True(); False(); }`, so a user redeclaration is a hard TYPE-6 error (enforced in the reference checker); the new branch reuses the same name-based invariant the existing match-arm code already relies on, adding no trust surface. bnot is fail-closed (exact-width name, exact arity, Bool operand); the reordered first-gate admits no new non-3-child shape except the gated bnot. The return flow enforces `value_type == return_type` by exact type-id equality on every path, and Clean requires a genuine Returns flow. Added regression `assert_reader_bool_returns_admitted` (positive Bool reader with bnot + True()/False() -> Clean; negatives: `bnot<u64>` -> Unsupported, non-returning path -> Unsupported, `own u8` return -> Unsupported). `make check` (all layers) and `make -C compiler check` green. RECORDED RESIDUALS: (1) the name-based True/False typing depends on TYPE-6 global enum-variant uniqueness holding for any program whose reader-Clean facts are trusted; the reference checker enforces it, but wfc's own front-end was not confirmed to run a whole-program TYPE-6 gate before facts are consumed — a pre-existing invariant (the shipped linear-profile codegen already relies on the same name-based True/False identification) worth an explicit wfc-side confirmation. (2) The `bor(u64,bool)` return gate in `run` is redundant with the widened `signature_valid` gate (belt-and-suspenders). STRATEGIC NOTE (flagged for owner direction on the next step): widening the return type admitted only 1 of 214 `own Bool`-returning functions — the binding constraint is the acyclic-flow + single-buffer signature, not the return type. Typing `True()`/`False()` is a special case of general enum-constructor typing, and `own Bool` return a special case of enum/struct return; the next frontier `lexer_scan_string` returns `own ScannedToken` and loops, forcing a general enum/struct-return + constructor + loop mechanism. Reaching the Phase-2 fixpoint (492 -> 0 unsupported) needs that general mechanism rather than more per-type shape profiles. Non-guarded surfaces only; no spec/conformance/oracle change and no owner approval required.

PHASE2-COVERAGE-PLAN (2026-07-18): the owner directed planning the path to the Phase-2 body-semantics classification fixpoint before building more per-shape profiles (the reader Bool-return slice added only 1 of 214 Bool-returning functions, confirming the return type is not the binding constraint). Characterized all 510 wfc source functions by structural requirement and set the coverage path (18 -> 510 classified) as SIX general capability families in dependency order. Evidence (measured over compiler/src/*.wf): return types 214 Bool / 174 unit / 62 u64 / 60 aggregate, and ALL 510 return `own` (zero borrow returns); control flow 81 functions loop (all with `set`; `continue` never used); mutation 181 `set`, 238 `writes`, all 174 unit-returners write; reborrow 194 pass a bounded `&uniq 'r deref(x)` (193 also write); signatures 256 buffer / 243 `&uniq` / 364 shared `&` / 233 multi-region; `box`/`arena` absent, `move`/`allocates` confined to 2 functions -- so NO new spec decision is needed for self-hosting coverage. The families: F1 general signatures + effect rows + read-only general body (+190; subsumes the reader/linear/scanner signature gates and folds the Bool/u64 return special-cases into general typing); F2 loops (`loop @label` + `break`) + local mutable `set` (+50; subsumes the scanner body profile); F3 unit-returning writers, mutation through `&uniq` + `writes` masks (+45); F4 bounded statement-scoped reborrow -- the analyzer side of the landed v0.7 OWN-5/6 rule, checker-side unimplemented (+148; the largest and highest-risk unlock, ~194 functions); F5 aggregate return + construction with payloads (+59); F6 `allocates(heap)` + `move` (+2 tail). Order is dependency-forced (reborrow unlocks nothing before write; loops nothing before set) and area-under-curve optimal. This is the CLASSIFICATION arc (Phase 2 step 1); whole-unit LLVM lowering is the separate step-2 track (only fixed-width lowers today). Hardest cluster: the ~40 parser `*_v2` functions need F1-F5 at once (final integration cluster). Each family is an optimizer fact channel and ships only after a hostile soundness review. Active slice: F1, first targets `frontend_lex_status_code` / `lexer_match3` / `llvm_buffer_fact_row_valid`, then `lexer_scan_string` as the first loop + aggregate proving ground. Corpus analysis is non-authoritative raw material; the exact per-slice count is pinned each slice per THE-PLAN. No code/spec/test change in this planning step.

F1-SLICE1-GENERAL-SIG-ENUM (2026-07-19): landed the first slice of coverage family F1 in the acyclic reader profile (compiler/src/semantic_reader.wf) — general signatures + general multi-variant enum `match` + an exact EFF-2 effect-reconciliation pass — taking the unit 510/18/492 -> 530/37/493/0 (19 functions newly clean; the +20 total growth is the new analyzer helper functions, themselves classified Unsupported). Self-parse 1,301,048 bytes / 258,976 tokens / 129,266 nodes. The slice generalizes the reader's signature gate from the narrow single-buffer shape to arbitrary `own` scalar (u8/u64/Bool) and by-value enum params, shared `&'r buffer<u8>` borrows, and multiple region params (pure or reads+traps effects, primitive/Bool return); and generalizes `match` from Bool-only to any enum via an exact-bijection exhaustiveness check (arm_count == variant_count AND each declared variant matched exactly once by globally-unique name [TYPE-6]). Newly clean (all Acyclic): the enum->code mappers frontend_lex_status_code / frontend_parse|ast_validation|globals|type|type_members|function_symbols_status_code, parser_token_kind_code, symbol_namespace_code, symbol_token_kind_code, symbol_lex_status_clean, symbol_lookup_tape_status_clean, semantic_prelude_chunk1..4, semantic_type_resolve_prelude_leaf_allowed, llvm_linear_operation_supported, llvm_buffer_fixed_width_supported. FACT-CHANNEL REVIEW (signatures are the broadest channel — they establish the optimizer's aliasing/effect trust): a 3-lens adversarial workflow plus an Opus re-review, a codex second opinion, and direct reads. The FIRST review empirically CONFIRMED (through the classifier) a false-clean the green gates missed: the generalized gate validated the effect row in ISOLATION from the body, admitting a `pure` function that `index`es a shared borrow (which reads its region and bounds-traps) and functions declaring reads('t) while reading 's — an EFF-2/EFF-3 violation and a real miscompile channel (the optimizer trusts pure/reads to reorder and elide traps). FIXED by adding an exact exhibited-effect pass (semantic_reader_op_traps / function_param_region / call_effectful / expr_effect / block_effect / effects_reconcile) computing the body's exhibited reads-regions + a traps flag per EFF-2 and requiring declared == exhibited both ways; analyze_call independently restricts every callee to exactly `pure` or `reads+traps` (so a traps-only / writes / allocates callee is rejected before reconciliation, closing the call-effect under-count vectors). The re-review found ONE residual (P3): an effectful user call in a MULTI-region function attributed its read to the first region rather than the buffer actually passed (bounded by staged region-retention debt; the reference checker admits the same; inert with no lowering yet). CLOSED fail-closed: a multi-region function that contains an effectful user call is Unsupported (effects_reconcile `multiple_regions` branch), pending region retention. Verified empirically: `two` (multi-region, indexes both buffers, no call) stays CLEAN; `hole` (multi-region, effectful call, region-arg/buffer mismatch) -> Unsupported; all 37 preserved. `make check` (all layers) and `make -C compiler check` green on main. RECORDED RESIDUALS: multi-region + effectful-call admission awaits region retention (then the fail-closed gate relaxes to precise per-buffer attribution); the reader's reads-row is a trustworthy region-disjointness fact only for single-region functions and index-based reads. Non-guarded surfaces only (semantic_reader.wf, semantic_unit.wf, test_semantic_unit.py, test_parser_expressions.py). PROCESS: implementation + the P3 fix were delegated to codex (gpt-5.6-sol) per the owner cost directive [[use-codex-for-delegation]]; codex's self-reported "gates green" reflected a transient build state, so the merge decision and every soundness verification stayed on the main loop (empirical classifier checks + adversarial review).

F1-SLICE2-TAPE-READS (2026-07-19): landed F1 slice 2 -- borrowed-struct-tape reads -- into the acyclic reader (compiler/src/semantic_reader.wf), taking the unit 530/37/493 -> 535/43/492/0 (6 new acyclic admits: parser_word_byte, parser_error_start, parser_error_end, llvm_scalar_next_is, llvm_scalar_resolves_to, llvm_scalar_ordinal_is; +5 total from new helper functions). Self-parse 1,321,014 bytes / 262,850 tokens / 131,144 nodes. The slice adds: (a) shared `&'r Struct` params -- struct type-id = decl_node + 2_000_000_000, disjoint from enum ids [1e9,2e9) and primitives (0..3), with the is_enum / enum_in_range checks bounded away from struct ids; (b) field-place typing (analyze_field_place / struct_field_type) for scalar (u8/u64/Bool) and enum fields of a borrowed struct, wired into analyze_expr; (c) a generalized analyze_index resolving the element via type_arg_id (u8/u64) over a base that is either deref(bufparam) [u8] or an AstFieldPlace field yielding buffer<u8|u64> (index_field_element), with an EXACT element match; (d) effect wiring -- a field read exhibits reads(region-of-struct-param) with NO trap, a typed index exhibits reads(region)+traps, and the signature gate now admits reads-without-traps rows. This is wfc's dominant data-access pattern index<T>(deref(tape).field, i) (811 index<u64> uses); only the 6 acyclic ones are admitted here -- the looping tape-readers stay on the scanner profile and are F2 work. Enum-element buffers (index<AstKind> etc.) are deferred to slice 2b-ii (fail closed now). FACT-CHANNEL REVIEW: codex STALLED THREE TIMES on this slice (empty diffs -- it exhausts its turn budget exploring the 3700-line analyzer even with a surgical spec), so it was implemented BY HAND on the main loop and verified with 44 adversarial programs through the classifier (15 by the author + 29 by an independent reviewer) plus a full independent Opus hostile review that returned GO / no false-clean. Correctly clean-or-rejected: element mismatch either direction (index<u64> on a u8 buffer/field and vice versa), pure-declared field read/index, non-buffer field index, `&uniq` struct param, nonexistent field, nested field path (deref(p).a.b), struct-typed field, buffer<enum> element index, multi-region field index with a wrong declared reads-region, and the existing buffer-param index (unchanged). The reviewer confirmed the effect walk visits every position a field read/index can appear (table-call operands and call arguments accept only literals/AstPlaceUse, so no effect-bearing node hides) and every id-space decode is range-disjoint and re-validated (struct_decl_valid / enum_decl_valid re-check kind + bound). `make check` (all layers) and `make -C compiler check` green on main. Added regression assert_reader_struct_field_and_typed_index; census 535/43/492 with COMPILER_CLEAN_ORDINALS + parser census (3380/47/3333) refreshed. RECORDED RESIDUALS (non-blocking): the reader trusts the upstream borrow-checker invariant that a shared `&'r` borrow is valid/live, so a scalar/enum field projection genuinely never traps (enforced upstream, not in this diff); the 1e9/2e9 id scheme assumes AST node counts stay far below 1e9 (true, defended by re-validation, but an implicit bound). Non-guarded surfaces only. PROCESS: this is the slice codex could not do -- see [[use-codex-for-delegation]] (codex handles small bounded fixes, stalls on large analyzer slices).

F1-FIELD-LEN (2026-07-19): added `len<u8|u64>` over a buffer field/param to the acyclic reader (compiler/src/semantic_reader.wf), taking the unit 535/43/492 -> 535/45/490/0 (2 new acyclic admits: source_span_valid, semantic_type_ast_columns_valid; no new helper functions -- inline branches). `len` is an AstTableCall (op-name "len", 2 children: type-arg + a buffer operand); the new branch in analyze_table_call requires the operand be a buffer place (deref(bufparam) [u8] or an AstFieldPlace buffer<T> field, reusing index_field_element) with the type-arg element EXACTLY matching the buffer element, result u64; expr_effect gains a `len` sub-branch exhibiting reads(region-of-operand) with NO trap (a length read is a fixed-offset load, no bounds check). Reuses the independently-reviewed index base-resolution + effect-region machinery from F1-SLICE2-TAPE-READS; verified adversarially through the classifier: `len<u64>(deref(t).u64field)` reads('s) -> CLEAN; the same declaring `pure` -> Unsupported (reads counted -- no under-declaration false-clean); `len<u8>` on a buffer<u64> field (element mismatch) -> Unsupported; `len` on a non-buffer scalar field -> Unsupported; `len<u8>(deref(bufparam))` -> CLEAN. `make check` (all layers) and `make -C compiler check` green on main. Added the len cases to assert_reader_struct_field_and_typed_index; census 535/45/490 with clean ordinals + parser census (3403/47/3356) refreshed. Enum-element `len`/`index` (over buffer<enum> fields -- the *_tape_shape_valid / *_columns_valid validators use `len` over buffer<SemanticTypeKind> etc.) is the next small field extension. Non-guarded surfaces only; a focused adversarial verification rather than a full new review, since the slice reuses reviewed machinery and adds one well-tested op.

F1-COVERAGE-HISTOGRAM (2026-07-19): measured what actually blocks the 490 unsupported wfc functions, to order the remaining capability families by real unlock rather than by guess. Method: a one-shot script walked each function's AST subtree and recorded which "blocker" construct families it contains, cross-checking each family against the 45 CLEAN functions to expose partial support. Key correction: AstConstructor covers nullary enum atoms (True(), AstKind()) which are ALREADY supported and appear in clean functions, so only ARGUMENT-carrying constructors (struct literals / payload variants) count as a ctor blocker -- that dropped the ctor bucket from 325 to 50. Results (blocker present among the 490 unsupported): call 403, region 198, write 197, uniqborrow 195, loop 96, ctor(with-args) 50, move 1. CLEAN cross-check (already partly handled by the scanner/linear profiles): call in 10 clean, loop in 3, write in 3 -- so loops/writes/calls are NOT all-or-nothing. PURE single-family buckets (a function whose ONLY listed blocker is that one family): call 132, write 30, ctor 5 -- and there is NO pure-loop bucket at all (loops always co-occur with write or call: loop+write 8, call+loop+write 48, ...). FINDING / re-prioritization: user-CALLS are the dominant unlock -- 132 functions blocked on calls alone plus the common factor in nearly every large combo -- while loops-first (the old family order) would unlock ~0 in isolation. A separate 42-function bucket contains ONLY table-call/field/deref/index/match (no loop/write/call/ctor/region/uniqborrow): the shape-validators and accessors (symbol_tape_columns_valid, semantic_body_kind_is, llvm_scalar_*, ...), blocked on enum-element index/len + enum equality -- confirmed by reading semantic_body_kind_is: `index<AstKind>(deref(ast).kinds, node)` then `ieq<AstKind>(observed, want)`, both rejected today because type_arg_id resolves only u8/bool/u64. RECOMMENDED ORDER (evidence-based, to surface to the owner): (1) F1-tail enum-element index/len + enum equality -- nearest pure-reader unlock of the 42-bucket, reuses the existing type_node_enum_id resolver and the reviewed exact-match machinery; (2) general user-calls (~132, highest leverage, needs an independent soundness review of callee-signature + effect propagation); (3) writes (~30 pure, F3); (4) reborrow region+uniqborrow (~108 in combo with call, F4); (5) loops last (F2) since no function is unlocked by loops alone. Enum equality is naturally Bool-safe: Bool's type-id is the primitive id 1, outside the enum range [1e9,2e9), so an is_enum range test admits `ieq<AstKind>` while still rejecting the illegal `ieq<Bool>`. This is a measurement/analysis gate (no code change); the scratch script was removed after use.

F1-ENUM-ELEMENT-PROTOTYPED-REVERTED (2026-07-19): implemented the enum-element index/len + enum-equality reader tail from the histogram plan, verified it SOUND, then discovered it unlocks ZERO wfc functions on its own and REVERTED it (tree returned to 810962c) rather than commit a 0-coverage half-slice. What was built (a line-anchored spec, in scratchpad `enum_element_spec.md`): a new leaf resolver `semantic_reader_leaf_enum_id` (token-valid + leaf + SymbolType lookup + enum_decl_valid -> enum id, kind-agnostic, mirroring `semantic_body_node_is_u8`); `symbols` threaded into `type_arg_id` / `analyze_index` / `analyze_table_call` / `index_field_element` (a closed call graph -- each reached only from `analyze_expr`, which already has `symbols`); `type_arg_id` and `index_field_element` fall through to the enum resolver after u8/u64; `analyze_index` widens the want-gate to `want_scalar OR want_enum` (range test); the binary-op prologue adds `operand_enum` (range test [1e9,2e9)) and equality uses `operand_scalar OR operand_enum` while ordered/arith/logical are untouched. VERIFICATION (17-case adversarial probe through the classifier): ALL soundness rejects pass -- `ieq/ine<Bool>` stays Unsupported (Bool id 1 is outside the enum range), `ige/ilt<Kind>` rejected (no enum ordering, ordered branch stays operand_scalar), element mismatch either direction rejected, mixed-enum operand mismatch rejected, under-declared pure index/len rejected, struct equality rejected (struct ids >= 2e9 fail the `< struct_base` high bound); the diff was read and matched the spec exactly. WHY IT UNLOCKS NOTHING: an `index<Enum>` result is an enum value, and the reader can only CONSUME it by (a) binding it to an enum-typed `let` or (b) returning it -- and BOTH are currently rejected (proven empirically: `let c: own Kind = a; ...` rejects at the binding type; `-> own Kind` rejects at the signature return gate). The lone enum capability that does work end-to-end, `ieq<Enum>` place-vs-place on params, is used by no function in the 42-bucket in isolation. So the 42 shape-validators/accessors (semantic_body_kind_is, llvm_scalar_*, ...) need enum-typed LETS + enum RETURNS as co-requisites; the enum-element index/len/equality plumbing is correct but inert without them. RELAUNCH PLAN: bundle enum-typed let bindings + enum (aggregate) return admission WITH the enum-element index/len/equality change as ONE function-unlocking slice, re-run the spec (codex regenerates it in ~5min), re-verify with the same probe, then measure the real unlock over the 42-bucket. CODEX BOUNDARY UPDATE [[use-codex-for-delegation]]: codex (gpt-5.6-sol) SUCCEEDED cleanly on this fully line-anchored spec in the SAME 3700-line semantic_reader.wf where it stalled 3x on the open-ended tape-read slice -- it made exactly the specified edits, respected the one-file constraint, and honestly reported the only failure as the expected pinned parser-census drift (3403->3409) rather than editing the guarded-adjacent test. Confirms the boundary is SPEC PRECISION, not file size: give codex line-anchored edits + invariants and it lands them; give it a design to discover in a huge file and it stalls. Non-guarded surfaces only; no committed code/spec/test change (analysis + reverted prototype only).
