F1-CALL-SUBSTITUTION-HARDENING (2026-07-19): closed a real v0.7 TYPE-5/OWN-12 false-CLEAN in the acyclic reader before widening user-call coverage. The original witness was a pure one-region callee `c<'r>(x: &'r buffer<u8>)` called from a two-region function as `c<'a>(x: b)`: type-id and mode matched, but the reader did not tie the shared actual's declaration region `'b` to the explicit substitution `'a`, so it classified the caller CLEAN. The repair keeps the existing bounded boundary (regionless or one-formal-region callees; pure or reads+traps; multi-region effectful calls, uniq, writes, and allocates remain fail-closed) and adds exact region provenance: the callee shared formal must name its sole declared region, the explicit argument must be a leaf REGIONID with exact arity/order and the caller's live region, and the shared actual must resolve to a validated parameter declaration whose region equals that explicit argument. Because this is an optimizer-fact channel, repeated independent adversarial reviews ran before shipping and exposed further structurally valid stale-tape false-CLEANs in the same ad-hoc callee scan; all were closed and pinned additively: nonleaf/wrong-kind region arguments; duplicate signature singleton nodes; malformed root/name/region/mode/effect/block shapes and token spellings; noncanonical direct-child order; symbol-resolved callee name disagreeing with the validated AST name; and duplicate formal texts paired with duplicate named arguments. The scan now checks exact `fn`, canonical signature order/cardinality/shapes/spellings, distinct contiguous formal names, callee-name == call-head, named argument name/order/count/type/mode, and exact formal/actual region substitution before returning a type. Correct controls for regionless/one-region pure and one-region reads+traps calls remain CLEAN. Exact compiler frontier is intentionally unchanged at 537 total / 51 CLEAN / 486 Unsupported / 0 rejected; parser region debt is 3,462 = 82 explicit + 3,380 staged omissions; self-parse is 1,350,260 bytes / 268,533 tokens / 133,857 nodes. Final independent correctness and performance verdicts are GO; `make check` and `make -C compiler check` are green, including model soundness 0, 262 conformance passes / 14 skips, codegen parity, and the exact 15-function native module. No generated user-code runtime changes; real whole-unit median showed no regression (46.766 ms vs 46.810 ms immediately before the duplicate-name hardening), optimized dylib/text allocations were unchanged, and the checks are allocation-free and bounded. RECORDED RESIDUAL: prior-formal duplicate detection is O(P^2 * name-length); current compiler maximum arity is 12 and 256 distinct formals measured 96.127 microseconds, so it is nonblocking but should be centralized or indexed later without weakening the check. Non-guarded surfaces only (`semantic_reader.wf`, additive compiler tests, parser census pin); no numbered specification, conformance verdict, oracle, or reference-semantics test changed.

F3-FLAT-WRITER-LITERAL-CONSTRUCTOR-SLICE (2026-07-19): advanced the exact writes-only F3 profile by only the two remaining pure RHS families needed by the next compiler helpers: canonical `u8`/`u64` literals and exact nullary `Bool` or user tag-only-enum constructors. User-constructor recognition is deliberately scoped to an exclusive-root field assignment and does not widen general expression typing: a bounded whole-unit AST scan requires exactly one direct variant with the constructor spelling, rejects duplicate or payload-like matches and malformed topology, proves the owning enum is tag-only, and returns the same nominal enum identity used by field typing. STAGE0-ENTRY-STACK-SLOT-CORRECTION (2026-07-19): complete compiler-source growth exposed a deterministic stage-0 lowering defect before the next F4 classifier slice could close. The facts-off LLVM for `lexer_run` executed a fixed-size `%ScannedToken` aggregate spill inside its token loop; LLVM stack allocation lifetime lasts until function return, so the native frame grew by 48 bytes per non-space token and eventually exhausted the stack even though source and output tape capacities remained valid. A focused additive regression first reproduced the defect on a struct-return call inside repeated control flow and now requires every fixed-size `alloca` in the function to precede the first body label. Stage 0 centralizes fixed-size stack-slot creation and emits those slots once at entry while leaving each initializing store at its original execution point; this also covers scalar locals, aggregate construction and call results, checked-condition observation, match result slots, and buffer-fill counters. Reuse is valid for the frozen stage-0 subset because these statically sized source bindings cannot escape their checked lifetime, and the change adds no optimizer fact, semantic authority, source check removal, or language rule. Raw-IR inspection of the repaired full lexer shows the call to `lexer_scan_one` with no stack-pointer decrement in the loop, and the complete source self-parse remains deterministic at 1,727,663 bytes / 348,731 tokens / 173,085 nodes. Existing generated LLVM examples were refreshed only for entry-block slot placement. `make check` and `make -C compiler check` are green after the correction, including unchanged spec-guard, all 91 rules, 278 conformance passes / 14 skips, zero accepted-program model-soundness violations, codegen parity, performance pins, and the complete 639-function compiler bootstrap. The toolchain design memory and roadmap cursor record the implementation fact; no numbered specification, conformance verdict, oracle digest, or existing reference-semantics test changed. The selected `byte_tape_emit_probe` F4 boundary remains next.

RUST-SOURCE-BINDING-FOUNDATION (2026-07-20): completed the first permanent Phase-2 Rust slice for exact kernel specification v0.8 without creating a disposable compiler or importing archived implementation code. The dependency-policed workspace contains exactly two safe-Rust library crates and no third-party package: `whitefoot-contract` owns judgment-free contracts and `whitefoot-verifier` depends only on it. The toolchain lock pins the 1.91 channel and minimal profile, rustc 1.91.1 commit `ed61e7d7e242494fb7057f2657300d9e77bb4fcb`, Cargo 1.91.1 commit `ea2d97820c16195b0ca3fadb4319fe512c199a43`, LLVM 21.1.2, rustfmt 1.8.0-stable, Clippy 0.1.91, and the exact component set; executable policy closes package membership, targets, edges, lints, compile-time inputs, dependency-lock identity, symlinks, build scripts, procedural macros, source paths, and build-override environment. `SourceBundle` preserves caller order, portable logical names, and exact raw bytes under explicit named ceilings; dense u32 `SourceId` values are documented as bundle-context coordinates rather than global identities, and validated half-open spans borrow the exact source file so equal-length cross-bundle substitution has no API. The version-1 `WFSOURCE` codec binds the exact specification SHA-256, source order, logical paths, and raw bytes with fixed big-endian framing; encoding preflights every per-source, aggregate-source, and whole-binding limit before allocation, while decoding rejects oversized, truncated, noncanonical, and trailing input under host-width-independent length handling. The independent verifier uses a separate positional traversal, has a private verified-state constructor, and exposes only narrow immutable verified-source views with no raw-binding downgrade. Token, tree, declaration, type, instantiation, check, and proof identities remain deliberately unfrozen until their canonical schemas exist.
